Headquarters of the Aviation Association Calls Meeting of Hotel Industry Fundraisers 128

Since the Shanghai Solicitation Team Headquarters of the Chinese Aviation Association started soliciting donations from the city's hotel industry based on 5% of their business income, the results have been excellent. However, some smaller hotels in categories C and D have not been diligent in their contributions. Therefore, at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, a meeting of the Hotel Industry Fundraising Committee was convened on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA to discuss the way forward. Attendees included Chuan Zhiyuan (Juelu Hotel), Chen Wenda (New World Hotel), Zhang Renliang (Wugong), Xu Wenzhao (Hongfu), Chen Yuanling (Nanjing), Cai Genyue (Ronghua), Zhu Linfeng (Zhongshan), Ren Heshan (Siming), Gao Weifu (Meng), Yang Yizhang (Xin Luming), Lu Youqiao (Zhongnan), Xi Rongpei (Da Hu), Yan Rongxiang (New Dongfang), Zhang Qiyuan (Da Zhonghua), Sun Qiuping, Zou Xieqing (Zhongzhou), Shi Xi (Dongfang), Wang Changgeng (Far East), Huang Renhe (Da Zhong), Shi Ming (Shenzhou), Li Jiemei (Da Shanghai), Yao Zhaoji (Chunjiang), Zhou Songxi, Yao Songnian, Gu Peiyuan, etc., as well as Li Dachao, Executive Director of the Team Headquarters; Zhang Yuliang, Chen Shuo, Zhu Shengyang, Lu Zhangyan, and Gu Shangrui, staff members; Chairman Li Dachao; and Recorder Chen Shuo. Chairman Li Dachao briefly reported that the hotel industry has been collecting donations according to business income since last year, thanks to the enthusiastic support and joint efforts of the industry association and various hotels, and the results have been very good. Even during the economic downturn, there has been monthly progress. The strength and spirit of the hotel industry are rare and commendable. The Team Leader expressed great pleasure and gratitude for the efforts of the hotel industry in this movement. The purpose of today's meeting is to discuss how to continue efforts in the future. After the fundraising began in the hotel industry, the effort by all the industry led to progress day by day. The average monthly revenue collected is around seven or eight thousand yuan. However, some smaller hotels in categories C and D have not been diligent in their contributions, and sometimes they collect and sometimes they stop. It is hoped that the fundraising committee will pay attention to this, and persuade them separately. As for category D hotels, if their business is indeed poor, they can follow alternative methods and make monthly donations. Even for small hotels, exemptions can be granted as appropriate to alleviate business difficulties. Furthermore, hotels that have not yet joined the industry association should be encouraged to join, so as to concentrate efforts, strengthen the organization, consolidate the foundation, and jointly seek the welfare of the industry. This office will do its best to assist, and so on. Subsequently, Chen Wenda, Gu Peiyuan, Gao Weifu, Sun Qiuping, Yao Songnian, and others from the hotel industry association spoke one after another, saying that they were very grateful for the Chairman's great remarks. Under the leadership of the China Aviation Association, the industry has worked hard to achieve today's results, and they are not complacent. In the future, they will be even more enthusiastic and work hard at all times to fulfill their national duties. As for the small number of hotels in categories C and D that are not diligent in collecting donations, they should be responsible for working with the China Aviation Association to send personnel to persuade them separately to collect seriously in order to fulfill their mission. Finally, the following matters were discussed: 1. Increase the promotion of solicitation: The Team Headquarters will list the collection status of each hotel and send it to the industry association for separate persuasion. 2. Assist the hotel industry association in expanding its solicitation of new members and strengthening the organization. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM.

Impersonating a Detective to Commit Robbery on the Road 132

Shen Fengming, from Chongming, was working as an informant for a Western detective at No. 26 Xuehuali Road, a property of the Public Works Department Company. On the morning of the 3rd of this month, at 12:00 PM, he went out shopping and encountered a bandit, Peng Yu Kui (27 years old, from Jiangbei), at the intersection of Kangti Road and Malong Road, who stopped him and falsely claimed, "I am Liu Ziqian, a detective from the police station. I am dispatched to inspect pedestrians." At that moment, Shen's friend, Zhu Hongqing, arrived. Peng pulled Shen into Lane 362, forcibly searched Shen's body, and robbed him of seven yuan and six jiao in cash. Shen realized that he had encountered a bandit and chased after him, blowing his whistle and shouting for thieves. A French Concession detective, Wu Lianrong, happened to pass by, heard the alarm, and caught up with Peng, recovered the stolen goods, and took him to the police station. Yesterday, he was escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District. First, the police officer presented the case and requested a postponement to allow the police to investigate whether the defendant had committed other crimes. After clarifying the case, he requested a trial. Judge Sun Penghan reviewed the report, questioned the defendant, and approved the postponement of the trial. The defendant was returned to custody.

Opening of the Sports Garden on the 10th 133

Yesterday's Reception for the Press

According to the Central News Agency, the Sports Garden at the intersection of West Sports Association Road is actively being arranged. Various ball fields, swimming pools, etc. have been completed one after another, and the opening will be held on the 10th of this month. Yesterday, the garden hosted the city's press for a tour, and business director Mr. Fang Lixiang and Mr. Zhang Yuliang reported. The internal equipment is detailed as follows:

Summer Resort

The Sports Garden is located at the intersection of West Sports Association Road, north of the Hongkou Swimming Pool. Public buses go directly to the entrance, making transportation very convenient. The garden covers dozens of acres, with lush grass and ancient trees. Based on its location, various ball games, entertainment, and places for banquets, dances, and rest are set up. Sitting in the breeze is truly a summer resort. The dance hall in the garden can accommodate hundreds of people and is the largest dance hall in Shanghai. The arrangement resembles a garden, with beautiful lighting. It is most suitable for daytime dancing. The cleanliness and deliciousness of its food and drink are all the more worthwhile.

Swimming Facilities

The swimming pool is located on the north side of the entrance. The area of the pool is smaller than the Hongkou Swimming Pool, but the sanitary equipment is more complete. There is also a medical room with eyewashers, sphygmomanometers, and various disinfectants for visitors to use. Two female nurses are hired to serve inside. Experts are also hired as instructors and coaches. Other facilities such as diving platforms, diving boards, slides, men's and women's changing rooms, shower rooms, storage rooms, and toilets are all very complete.

Various Entertainments

In terms of sports and entertainment, there are golf and hockey fields, ice skating, donkey riding, etc. Hockey is already a popular game in Europe and America. Although some Chinese people are familiar with this game, there has been no establishment of such a ball field. The garden's equipment is truly pioneering. There is also a maze, with a novel design that is captivating. Other new forms of entertainment are all original creations in China.

Purpose of Establishment

According to the person in charge, Mr. Sou, speaking to the reporter, the garden was originally the private garden of Mr. Zhou Suqun, a wealthy merchant from Guangdong. In view of the progress of construction in the city center and the relatively quiet market in the northern part of Shanghai, and the existing entertainment venues are all concentrated in the western part of Shanghai, in order to develop the market in this area, he specially opened the private garden and spent tens of thousands of yuan to set up various entertainments for the public to enjoy after work. After the opening, the entrance ticket will only cost four jiao, and with the ticket, one can enjoy one of the various entertainments in the garden with preferential treatment. The food and drink in the area are especially inexpensive and beautiful, and so on.

Collision of Sailing Ships Causes Disaster 135

The pottery cargo ship Tao Jisheng recently loaded bricks and tiles in the interior and transported them to Yinxiang Port to unload. In order to make up for lost time, it was sailing day and night. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, it was sailing near the Liu River in the Southern Huangpu River. It was sailing fast with the wind. The Zhu Gendi ship, loaded with sugar and groceries from Shanghai to Jiahu, was also sailing with the wind. When the two ships saw each other, they both steered to avoid a collision. However, due to the strong wind and waves, they could not avoid it in time. The two ships collided violently. The Zhu ship was hit and retreated more than ten feet. The ship immediately capsized on the shore, and the people on board all fell into the water. The Tao ship was larger. There was a hole in the bow of the ship. Tao and his group also fell into the water at that time. The Tao ship's crew immediately lowered a sampan to rescue them. Tao and Zhu and their partners were rescued on the spot, but one crew member from each of the Tao and Zhu ships was missing. Zhu immediately hired a boat to try to right the ship. However, the sugar and groceries in the ship were all wet, and the bow of the ship was damaged. The two people came to Shanghai yesterday to report to the cargo owners and negotiate. Both sides have their own reasons and are unwilling to take responsibility. However, Zhu believes that the loss of the ship and cargo was great due to the collision and has detained the Tao ship, intending to sue for compensation for the loss.

Wife Who Fled Eight Years Ago Meets Again 136

Lu Tan does not want to go back with her husband, Lu Senlin.

At 11:05 PM the night before last, police officer Li Lanyuan, badge number 34 of the Zhabei Zhongxing Road Police Station, was on duty on Gonghe Xin Road when a man named Lu Senlin brought a woman, Lu Tan, claiming that Tan was his legal wife and had fled eight years ago, etc. Officer Li brought them both to the station and transferred them to the Xinzha Sub-bureau. Wang Chongren, an officer of the bureau, questioned Lu Senlin, who stated that he was 31 years old, from Pudong, lived at No. 444 Gonghe Xin Road, and worked as a cook. Lu Tan was his legal wife and had fled eight years ago. Recently, she returned to his home and deceived his 12-year-old son, named Cai Bao, and hid him. He requested that Tan be ordered to live with him again, go back with him, and hand over Cai Bao. Lu Tan stated that she was 32 years old this year and had fled eight years ago because her husband beat her. Cai was indeed her biological son, but she did not know where he was at the moment. Today she came with her employer. Her employer lives at No. 16 Huanlong Road in the French Concession. Today she cannot go back with him. She has been helping in this employer's house for five years, so she wants to ask her employer to make the decision. Moreover, she has more than 200 yuan in debt that has not been cleared up, and so on. After reviewing the statements, the interrogating officer believed that the case concerned a marital dispute and that the sub-bureau was not in a position to handle it without authorization. Therefore, he ordered that they be sent to the Public Security Bureau for a decision.

New New Garden: Female Hostess Jumps From Building, Dies Before Reaching Hospital 141

A Hangzhou woman named A Feng, real name Fu Zhen, 18 years old, lived with only her elderly mother. Due to difficult living conditions, she was introduced to work as hostess number 67 in the rooftop garden of the New New Company on Nanjing Road. She was usually very lively, so her colleagues got along well with her. She was also naturally charming and innocent, like a young woman who had not experienced much of the world. However, for some unknown reason, this fragile girl suddenly became pessimistic and conceived a desire to end her life. At around 8:40 PM last night, when tourists were bustling about, A Feng suddenly ran to the balcony of the rooftop garden near the intersection of Nanjing Road and Guangxi Road, climbed over the cement railing, stepped over the iron fence, and threw herself down to the street below, committing suicide. At the time, no one noticed, so it went undetected. It was only when a patrolman at the street intersection saw her that an alarm was raised. He rushed forward to check and found that her head, feet, hands, and other parts of her body were all seriously injured. She barely had any breath left, so he urgently reported to the Old Zha gate police station, which rushed her to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, due to the severity of her injuries, she died shortly after arriving at the hospital. Her body has been sent to the morgue for examination. Her name and address could not be immediately determined because the garden's tea sales were not directly managed by the company but were contracted out to a man named Shen Changgeng. As for the reason for her suicide, her colleagues said it was probably due to the pressure of making a living, or perhaps it was due to romantic love or family misfortune. They are currently searching for her family to handle the funeral arrangements.

Shanghai Ferry Company: Complete Sale of Property, Eight Company Motorboats Sold for 24,000 Yuan, Contract Signed on the 1st 142

According to the Datong News Agency, the Shanghai Ferry Company sold all of its assets and business rights to Song Wenkui, who was previously employed by the British company Moutai Yanghang on Hankou Road, on the first of this month. Details are listed below:

Eight Motorboats: The company has been established for more than three years and is a joint-stock venture. The general manager is Mr. Gu Fujiang, and the office is located at No. 244 Zhonghui Building. The business office is located at the floating pier on Jiujiang Road. There are a total of eight small motorboats (two of which are mortgaged to the company by the American company Shishi He Yanghang).

Complete Sale: The motorboats are temporarily rented to shipping companies to transport passengers to and from Shanghai-bound foreign ships berthed at the floating docks on the Huangpu River, which is a major part of the business. Due to the impact of the widespread economic downturn, the business has been poor, so the shareholders decided to sell all of the company's assets and business rights.

Contract Signed: The buyer of all the company's assets is Mr. Song Wenkui, who previously worked for the British company Moutai Yanghang (specializing in transshipment business) on Hankou Road (his position was equivalent to that of a Chinese manager). The selling price is 24,000 yuan. The contract was signed by both parties on July 1 at the law firm of Xu Shihao at No. 33 Sichuan Road, and the buyer paid the seller 8,000 yuan in advance. The remaining amount will be paid in full after one month.

Foreign Company Dominance: According to statistics, there are four companies operating ferry services in Shanghai. In addition to the Shanghai Ferry Company, which sold its property rights this time and is wholly Chinese-owned, the other three are American company Shishi He, Huangpu (British company Moutai Yanghang), and Tingmao (also British). Therefore, the complete sale of Shanghai Ferry Company's property rights is deeply regrettable to outsiders.

Chen Zhaoshun, a native of Shaoxing residing at No. 90 Guishi Lane, Tiantong Road, North Fujian Road, impersonated a representative of the Public Works Department Fire Brigade on October 15th of last year. He sent his apprentices, Ding Zhiming and Xu Changhai, to follow and investigate, but they soon lost track of him. Therefore, he requested permission to postpone the trial to investigate whether the defendant was a public servant. Cause of Death of Boy in Xiaobang Lane: Three Scavenging Children Robbed Silver Necklace, Little Dog Lost His Life in Vain 146

Yesterday's newspaper reported that the body of a 14-year-old boy, Su Xiaogouzi, was found in Xiaobang Lane, Wangdao Port, Gaochang Temple, South Shanghai. He had been murdered and had knife wounds on his head. He was rescued by the police, sent to Shanghai Hospital, and died after ineffective treatment. It is now known that the deceased, Su Xiaogouzi, was 14 years old, a native of Xinghua, Jiangbei. He usually carried a bamboo basket to scavenge for scraps. Because his parents loved him, he had worn a silver necklace (worth about three yuan) since he was a child. The day before yesterday (the 2nd), after finishing his meal at home, Xiaogouzi carried his basket out as usual. Unexpectedly, he met with this tragedy. According to people, the cause of the tragedy was greed for money. Three other scavengers, older than the deceased, ganged up on him to snatch the silver necklace from Xiaogouzi's neck. Xiaogouzi refused to let go and resisted. However, he was no match for the gang, and they forcibly snatched it and tried to escape. Xiaogouzi cried and shouted, "I know you! I won't let you get away with this!" When the bad kids heard this, they feared the consequences and, without considering the consequences, immediately turned back, pulled out sharp blades, and slashed wildly at Xiaogouzi's head. Then, they used ropes to tighten around Xiaogouzi's neck. Finally, they dragged Xiaogouzi to a small river and drowned him in the mud. The stories vary, and no one knows for sure. Then, the police discovered that Xiaogouzi had not completely died, so they tried to rescue him and rushed him to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. The boy's mother, Su Chen, heard the news and rushed to the hospital. She confirmed that it was her son. Unfortunately, Xiaogouzi was seriously injured and could not speak. He only used gestures to describe how he was robbed of his necklace by the children. Yesterday morning, Zhang Hongxun, the local headman, reported the case to the local court and requested an autopsy. In the afternoon, Commissioner Lei Binzhang and Inspector Yi Zhiming arrived at the court. The autopsy revealed that the deceased Su Xiaogouzi had three knife wounds on the back of his head, his skull had been shattered, and there was a knife wound in his right eye socket, penetrating deep into the brain. There were also marks on his neck from being strangled. It was confirmed that he died from his injuries. The death certificate was filled out, and the family was instructed to prepare a coffin and wait for the arrest and punishment of the murderers. It is astonishing that a mere silver necklace could cost someone their life. No wonder glittering gold attracts so much attention and can lead to death.

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Announces the Recovery of the Dateli Wharf 148

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has been planning to take over the Dateli Company for a long time. Recently, both parties reached an agreement. The bureau sent personnel to take over. The process is recorded as follows:

Implement Reorganization Plan: Except for the Dateli Company Wharf, all private wharves in the South Shanghai Wharf area have been taken back by the city in accordance with the reorganization plan. In November 1933, in order to implement the wharf reorganization plan and reorganize the traffic on the outer roads, the Public Utilities Bureau, the Public Works Bureau, and the Land Bureau decided to take back the company's private wharf.

Decide on Recovery Method: After the company's private wharf is taken back, it will be reorganized and rented to the company or other companies by the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities to increase the city's revenue and improve the city's appearance. This decision was approved by the bureau and filed with the municipal government.

Estimate Wharf Assets: The price of the wharf was jointly determined by the Public Utilities Bureau, the Public Works Bureau, and experts, and discussed and decided with the company. The floating wharf, floating bridge, cement part, and the area occupied by the sheds were estimated to be worth 30,000 yuan.

Handle Takeover Procedures: After the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities and the company reached an agreement on all takeover procedures, on June 24th, the bureau dispatched Secretary Kong Huai and Technical Officer Li Yongqing to the company to take over the wharf assets and its ancillary buildings. The wharf price of 30,000 yuan was also paid to the company by the bureau. In addition, the company paid 1,000 yuan for outstanding dredging fees, line fees, and 1,357 yuan and 2 jiao for beach and public land rent.

Continue to Rent the Wharf: After the Dateli Wharf was taken back, the company requested to rent it. The amount of the wharf rental fee and deposit has been negotiated between the company and the bureau. A wharf rental contract was signed on June 24th, and the rental began on that day. All procedures have been completed by the bureau and reported to the municipal government for filing.

Implement Reorganization Work: The houses attached to the wharf protrude into the embankment line and occupy the road surface of the outer roads, which greatly hinders vehicle traffic. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities and the Public Works Bureau previously planned to draw a straight line from the garbage wharf to the Dangguan Wharf, which would be the embankment line. All sheds within the embankment line will be demolished. Now that the takeover of the Dateli Wharf has been completed, the sheds within the embankment of the Dateli Wharf, together with the Minnan Wharf, will be demolished. The road surface will be widened, and the embankment line between the Dateli and Minnan wharves will be extended outward.

Wang Xianggu Writes Letter to Thank Taxpayers' Association: The Public Works Department's Tax Collection Lawsuit Resolved, The Taxpayers' Association Upholds Justice and Supports Citizens, The Public Works Department's Administration Demonstrates the Spirit of the Rule of Law 149

Lawyer Wang Xianggu, a taxpayer in the Public Concession, wrote to the Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association yesterday, saying: "I am writing to inform you that the taxpayer was cut off his phone line due to the Public Works Department's tax collection office overcharging general tax. I sent two letters to your association, requesting that you forward them to the department to immediately restore the phone service and compensate for all losses, and so on. Since the second letter was sent, more than a year has passed, and the department has not replied. Instead, it filed a lawsuit in the Shanghai First Special District Local Court last autumn to recover the tax. The taxpayer believed that the department's illegal phone cut-off affected the legal interests of the entire citizenry of the concession. To maintain the taxpayer's position, he filed a counterclaim, demanding compensation for damages. The department argued in the litigation process that the counterclaim could not be filed. The judge in the first instance ruled in favor of the department. The taxpayer, based on the interpretation of the former Supreme Court's Tong Zi No. 97, argued that although the plaintiff was not subject to our country's jurisdiction under the treaty, it should not be treated as an ordinary defendant in the case of a counterclaim. He filed an appeal. After several court hearings, the department was willing to waive the tax and offset the losses, withdrawing the original lawsuit. The taxpayer also withdrew the appeal. The two parties jointly petitioned the court to dismiss the case, and the court issued a notice approving it yesterday. The taxpayer is grateful that the resolution of this phone cut-off incident is largely due to the department's willingness to admit its mistakes. But it cannot be separated from the efforts of your association to uphold justice, support the citizens, and be worthy of the voice of the taxpayers of the concession. It is hoped that the department will administer according to the law from now on, demonstrating that it is the only municipal organization that embodies the spirit of the rule of law. Work together with your association, which represents the public opinion, to benefit not only the taxpayers but also the citizens of the concession. Because the incident has come to an end, I am writing to inform you of the process and thank your association, and I ask that you close the case. Yours sincerely, Wang Xianggu, taxpayer of the Shanghai Concession."

He Fu Petitions the American Court to Order Raven to Return the Gift Money, Xie Fuzi, Manager of the American Eastern Bank, Returns to Shanghai 150

The *China Press* reported that yesterday (the 3rd) afternoon, Mr. He Fu, the liquidator of the American Feng Bank and three other companies, petitioned the American Court in China again, ordering Mr. Raven to return 135,000 taels of silver that the American Eastern Bank and the Puyi Real Estate Company had each given him in 1932, plus interest at 6% per annum from the date of receipt to the date of return. He Fu claimed that the board of directors of the two companies passed resolutions to grant the silver that were worded the same as those passed by the board of directors of the American Feng Bank, saying that Mr. Raven had served faithfully for a long time without receiving any salary or other remuneration. It is now found that Mr. Raven was paid a monthly salary of 2,000 yuan for some time before the board of directors of Puyi Real Estate Company passed the resolution, and he continued to receive it after the resolution was passed. Therefore, his acceptance of the gift was improper and deceptive. The resolutions passed by the two companies stipulated that the gift would be written off in the books over six years. Judging from the situation, Raven must have known that the company was empty and on the verge of bankruptcy at the time. The two newly filed cases do not require Raven to increase the security deposit, because the bond guaranteed by the American Feng Bank case is sufficient to prevent him from leaving China. These three cases will not be heard in one or two weeks, because Mr. Hillmiche, the chief judge of the American Court, is currently handling cases in North China and cannot return to Shanghai for a while. He Fu also mentioned yesterday the liquidation of the Tianjin branch of the American Feng Bank, saying that he had received some money from the branch's fraud. As for the liquidation of the Hong Kong branch of the American Eastern Bank, it should naturally be handled by the American court. The same is true for the company in Manila. Therefore, he cannot interfere with the affairs of the Shanghai liquidation office. He is very busy now. Although today is American Memorial Day, he will still be working as usual. The bank's supplies, such as electric fans and typewriters, are now being sold cheaply to raise more cash. The *Continental Daily News* reported that Mr. Xie Fuzi, the former manager of the American Eastern Bank, took leave to return to the United States at the beginning of this year. He set off to return to China last month and arrived in Shanghai the night before last. While in the United States, he had not heard that the company had gone bankrupt. When he happily returned to the company yesterday morning, he found that it was closed for liquidation. He was greatly dismayed. He told people that if he had known that the company had closed, he would not have returned to Shanghai in such a hurry.

Jiaotong University Research Institute Proves the Advantages of the Appler Light Bulb 152

Among domestic light bulbs, the Appler brand is often the oldest and largest. The light bulbs produced are also the most energy-saving, durable, and have accurate lighting. Now, after testing by the Research Institute of National Jiaotong University, Report No. 105 states that the Appler light bulb has the following advantages: (1) After 12 light bulbs were continuously powered for 1,000 hours, the filaments were not damaged, and the candlepower did not drop below 80%. (2) The power consumption rate of light bulbs with the same standard code is very uniform. (3) The power consumption rate per candlepower and the number of lumens per watt meet the standards. (4) The degree of candlepower reduction after continuous power for 1,000 hours also meets the standards. Therefore, users in various places have recently been sending letters and telegrams to order, and although they have been jealous and slandered by the industry, they can now produce in large quantities.

Record of the Opening Trial of the Lu Guixing Murder Case: Complex Situation Still Requires Investigation; Defendants Remanded for Further Questioning 155

Lu Guixing, a 45-year-old man from Anhui, lived in the Triangle Street of the South City. He had previously served as a detective for the Public Security Bureau. After being dismissed from his position in June of last year, he had been unemployed at home. In the spring of this year, Lu's apprentice, Chen Liaotou, and Fan Guangyu, Gao Yusheng, Shu Jinbao, etc., had a conflict due to contracting the shoulder-carrying of foreign pine work for the Renhe Lumber Company. As a result, Lu intervened and mediated, and the matter was settled. On June 4th (i.e., the fourth day of the fifth lunar month), Fan Guangyu invited Chen Liaotou to Lu Jiabang's No. 1 Teahouse to settle the remaining profits. Chen Liaotou then accompanied Lu Guixing to the teahouse at 2 PM to negotiate. However, they disagreed and started fighting. As a result, Lu Guixing was stabbed to death. His wife, Lu Li, sued in court, and the local court sent personnel to verify the coffin and burial. Meanwhile, the police successively arrested the murderers Li Guitian, Fan Guangyu (who was also cut in the left arm), Shu Sanbao, and others, and detained them for investigation. It is now known that this case has been thoroughly investigated by Prosecutor Lei Binzhang, who has prosecuted the case in the criminal court for causing death by injury. At 10 AM yesterday, Judge Shao Qinzhi specially opened the Third Tribunal to hear the case. First, the deceased's wife, Lu Li, testified, stating that she was 42 years old and that her husband, Lu Guixing, was stabbed to death by Li Guitian and others. She demanded justice. Next, Chen Liaotou testified, stating that he was 40 years old and from Gaoyou. On the fourth day of the fifth lunar month, he and Lu Guixing sent wages to the teahouse, but Fan Guangyu and others, without asking the reason, attacked them with stools. Seeing that the situation was not good, he ran away to avoid danger. Fan Guangyu testified that he was 44 years old and from Shandong, working as a foreman at the Renhe Lumber Company. He, Chen Liaotou, Lu Guixing, and others signed a contract, stipulating that if they earned 100 yuan, Lu Guixing wanted to deduct 20 yuan. On that day, Lu Guixing and others had ambushed many thugs and forcibly deducted the 20 yuan remuneration. He and others refused to accept this, which led to a fight. In desperation, he resisted with a stool. His arm was injured by Chen Liaotou with an iron rod. As for how Lu Guixing died, he did not know and asked for investigation. Li Guitian testified that he was 39 years old and from Shandong, working as a small laborer. His testimony was the same as Fan Guangyu's. Shu Sanbao testified that he was 28 years old and from Xinghua, Jiangbei. On the morning of the fourth day of the fifth lunar month, he went to Tangqiao for something and did not return home until 4 PM. Lu Guixing's apprentice came to his house and said that "Three Companies" (referring to the contract signed by the three of them) had killed someone and asked him to pay 400 yuan for funeral expenses. He believed that this share was handled by his brother, Shu Jinbao, and had nothing to do with him. He refused to pay, so he was arrested late at night and asked for investigation. The judge, after hearing the testimony, believed that the case was complex and still needed investigation. Therefore, he ordered all defendants to be remanded. Chen Liaotou was still released on bail to await further trial.

Hereafter, all bureaus shall temporarily stop accepting and sending parcels containing saccharin, saccharin powder, lactose, coffee essence, caffeine, etc." This is hereby announced for your information.

General Situation of the Anglo-Swiss Condensed Milk Company 157

The manufacture of condensed milk was invented by Mr. Borden in the United States as early as 1856. However, its manufacture in Switzerland was pioneered by Mr. Page, who was the American Consul to Switzerland at that time. On August 6, 1866, he founded the Anglo-Swiss Condensed Milk Company in Switzerland, with a capital of 100,000 francs. This was gradually increased to over 20 million francs, and factories were established in Switzerland, the United Kingdom, Norway, the United States, and other places.

The Nestlé Milk Powder Factory was founded in 1875 in Vevey, Switzerland, for the purpose of taking over the milk powder workshop established by the chemist Henri Nestlé. From 1878 onwards, this company also manufactured Nestlé brand condensed milk. The company progressed very rapidly, and soon its activities expanded to foreign countries such as Spain, Norway, the United Kingdom, and the United States. The initial capital of the company was 1 million francs, which was increased to 2 million francs in 1881. In 1904, the company entered into a contract with the Swiss Chocolate Factory to manufacture Nestlé brand milk chocolate, and invested 1 million francs in that company, thus increasing its capital from 2.5 million francs to 3.5 million francs. At the same time, the company also became the sole agent for the export of all brands of chocolate produced by that factory in the United Kingdom.

The current Anglo-Swiss Condensed Milk Company was formed in 1905 by the merger of the Nestlé Factory and the Anglo-Swiss Condensed Milk Company. Since then, its business has flourished. New factories have been established in various important producing countries. Today, the company's business has spread all over the world. On the one hand, sales offices have been established, and on the other hand, many independent companies have been entrusted with managing sales. The company's capital increased to 160 million francs after the merger in 1905. After the European War, the world economy declined greatly, and the company was also affected, suffering heavy losses. Therefore, it had to reduce its capital to 80 million francs. After this reorganization, the company's products were well-known, and it was able to develop greatly in the following years. In 1929, the company also acquired the Peter-Cailler-Kohler Swiss Chocolate Factory. This merger was based on a stock exchange calculation, i.e., each share of Anglo-Swiss Company stock worth 200 was exchanged for four shares of the above-mentioned company, each worth 100 . As a result, the company's capital increased by 17.5 million to 97.5 million francs, and the Anglo-Swiss Condensed Milk Company became the world's largest manufacturer of condensed milk and chocolate. This development has increased, and its activities have also expanded to other products, such as milk powder and etc. Currently, the company has 6,000 employees and 17,000 workers. The board of directors has twelve members in Switzerland, with Mr. Davel as the chairman.

Special Feature: Liu Haisu Reports on His European Tour (6) 172

This exhibition of modern Chinese paintings and large-scale works from various countries is not only a powerful cultural dissemination in our country but also an important contribution to the Western academic community. It has also aroused the interest of young scholars from various countries in studying Chinese painting. For example, Dr. Contag from Germany and Ms. Sebeke from England have already visited China. The Bali Art Museum in Berlin has opened a hall dedicated to modern Chinese paintings. All these things have created a new record in the history of international culture. The benefits gained are also worth mentioning, roughly as follows:

(1) Changing the Previous Misconceptions of European Scholars: Oriental scholars and art historians in various European countries consistently praise the value of ancient Chinese art in their writings. However, they believe that there is no art to speak of in China after the Yuan and Ming dynasties. This preconceived notion holds that the splendid and beautiful art of ancient China has become a thing of the past. In addition, the government of our Eastern neighbor has repeatedly allocated huge sums of money in recent years to vigorously promote its modern art, seemingly claiming the highest position in the East. Therefore, Europeans generally regard China as a thing of the past. Regarding modern Eastern art, they only know Japan and do not know China. This has even created the fallacy that China has no modern culture. The exhibition of modern paintings in various countries has given scholars from various countries a deep interest in research and provided people from various countries with an opportunity for universal contact. It has changed the previous misconceptions of various countries and made them deeply believe that Chinese art is constantly progressing. They admire and learn from it. Such discussions have been published in newspapers in various countries. Here are a few excerpts: On May 16, 1934, the German "East and Wheel Report" published a lengthy article reviewing the Chinese modern painting exhibition, which included a passage saying, "We used to say that Chinese painting is nothing more than a weak review of ancient masterpieces, and that ancient paintings are far-sighted and insightful. How frivolous and superficial is this view! Naturally, even with the paintings of famous modern Chinese painters such as Liu Haisu, Qi Baishi, Ren Bonian, and Wu Changshuo, it is not enough to surpass the masterpieces of the Song and Yuan dynasties, just like the works of modern German masters compared to Dufort Holdim or Gounwald. Here, we can't say which is higher or lower, but we must pay attention to the differences, because the creative goals of today's Chinese painters are different from those of the past, and they have new tendencies and new expressions. This can only be discovered by studying carefully, but I am not only talking about its influence by Europe. Soon, the European art scene will be influenced by it..." In addition, the British art authority, Binyon, also said in the preface to our book exhibition, "European and Western collectors and connoisseurs all love ancient and rare objects, so there are many barriers to modern Chinese art. They all believe that this art, which has been passed down for two thousand years, has become a thing of the past. Today, thanks to the efforts of artists, it is confirmed that Chinese painting has been revived, and it is not only continuing its long history, but also able to break free from the old Chinese style and absorb the essence of European and Western famous paintings. Mr. Liu Haisu once came to Europe and the West to study art, and he has a deep understanding of Chinese ink painting and Western oil painting techniques. He is proficient in using them freely and can be compared with modern European masters. This time, he brought paintings to Europe for exhibition. His personal masterpieces are magnificent and elegant, and they are truly extraordinary, which is especially admirable. The masterpieces in the exhibition, whose style and themes are in line with Chinese customs and can open up new paths, Western superficial views often regard innovation as creation, while Chinese writers do not all follow the ancients, because the rebirth of art lies in the great personality of the artist, renewing his vision and soul, and revitalizing customs, has completed his mission..." Lourence Binyon is a British master of literary criticism who has studied Chinese art for forty years and has written books such as "Painting of the East" and "History of Chinese Art". He once said that Chinese art had declined after the Yuan and Ming dynasties, but now he has changed his tune. (To be continued)

Snippets 174

— (Jin Xiongzi)

A man sitting in a rickshaw can only accommodate up to two people, but a woman sitting in a rickshaw can sometimes pile up to three, which shows that urban women are indeed light-boned.

In the hearse, you can often see a few pretty smiling faces with rouge and powder.

The most unsightly thing on a person is the face of a gentleman and the feet of a Jiangbei grandma.

From a husband's clothes, you can see the diligence or laziness of his wife.

Youth is like the green grass of spring, adulthood is like the peony of March; old age is the remnant chrysanthemum of autumn; and old age is the withered leaves waiting to fall.

Weary Mood 175

— Hu Tianyu

I feel the deepest weariness for drifting.

I need rest now. I think, as long as there are three rooms and a courtyard; one room as a study, one as a bedroom, and one as a guest room; in the courtyard, I can plant some favorite flowers and plants, and place some exquisite bonsai. Every day, I go from the bedroom to the study, and from the study to the courtyard. When friends come, I can sit with him in the guest room and talk. In this peaceful and elegant environment, I will become a happy person. My lifelong hope is this, and when will this be realized? Alas!

I am tired, yes, really tired. But what is the use of being tired?

In the blue sky, the birds circling, looking for food, flying all day, making it feel unbearably tired, but before it has filled its stomach, it has no way to settle comfortably in the nest in the woods.

This suggests that my weariness can only be endured and cannot rest in my ideal comfortable nest.

I heard the girl's delicate voice singing: "You have been busy for many years, until today... You are too tired, you should rest!... My Darling! Don't move, don't move, rest for five minutes"! However, I can't even rest for five minutes, even though I am so tired!

Say less! Tomorrow, tomorrow I will continue my drifting!

Song and Dance in Southeast Asia 176

— Intention

Although Chinese song and dance have not completely left the stage of immaturity, there has been significant progress from children's opera to adult song and dance, and from fairy tale materials to realistic plots.

The year before last, the Meihua Troupe performed song and dance dramas such as "Love School" in the Nanyang Islands, with a total business income of more than 300,000 shields (equivalent to more than 600,000 Chinese currency), which aroused the song and dance fever of the Nanyang masses. Therefore, domestic song and dance troupes have unanimously invested in Nanyang. Currently, the Meihua, Qiangwei, Wanhua, and Sanban troupes have arrived in Nanyang, and the Yinhua, Hudie, and Lihua troupes are on the way. Therefore, the domestic song and dance news is silent. Now, I will briefly report on the recent situation of the three major groups that have performed in various parts of Nanyang to those who care about song and dance.

Meihua: Departed last November, via Singapore, Siam, and the Malay Peninsula, and is now performing in Penang. The main characters are Zhang Xianlin, Cai Yiming, Xu Canying, Fan Lixiang, etc. The main programs are "A Spring Dream" and "Playing". It has a strong appeal and is enthusiastically welcomed everywhere. In Siam, the business income in one day was more than 5,000 shields, and the actors were paid five times their salary, breaking the Meihua Troupe's all-time box office record. The grand occasion can be imagined.

Qiangwei: Departed this February, via Hong Kong, Kowloon, Annam Di'an, and Siam, and is now performing in Singapore. It has the Pan sisters, Wenxia and Wenjuan, who once caused a sensation in Nanyang, as its pillars. Its appeal is also quite strong. In Annam Di'an, the box office was undiminished for a month, which was due to the Pan sisters' beauty and art. The main programs are "A Spring Dream" and "Transformation", etc. Pan Wenjuan's "Red Dance" and "Toe Dance" were also very popular for a while.

Wanhua: Departed this March, via Singapore, Malay, and Sahara, and is now in Saigon, Annam. The female actors are quite complete, with 16 people including Zhang Lijuan and Li Meimei, but it is calling with no famous character, its business income is inferior to Meihua and Qiangwei.

Bathing 177

Record of the Orchid of the Valley 178

— Shi Yuan

The orchids in the empty valley always emit a strange fragrance, which is a blessing unique to the disciples of Yufu. Urban people cannot enjoy it, and even if they are occasionally moved to a crowd, they do not make a startling sound or offer a flattering look. However, if people approach them, they will naturally feel happy. Isn't art the same? I once went to Songjiang and visited the New Songjiang Society. The Songfeng Painting and Calligraphy Society happened to gather there. The gentlemen expressed their aspirations and entrusted their lofty feelings to painting and calligraphy. The dazzling array of treasures made me sigh that they were enough to make Yufu proud in this world. And recently, this society suddenly quietly exhibited its superb structures in the northern commercial market of the New World. The viewers rubbed shoulders and stepped on each other's heels. Is this also the orchid of the valley, not seeking to be known by others, but people come to it themselves? During my spare time, I often linger and admire it. I write down a glimpse to tell those who have not seen it, and to confirm it with those who have already seen it.

The landscapes of Fei Longding, Zhang Shutong, Zhuocheng brothers, Wang Shilin, and Min Ruizhi are full of spirit and harmony, and they look like old hands. Young painters such as Yu Xiaolian's landscapes are elegant, ancient, and can be called the authentic school of Songjiang. The ladies also got the essence of Yuhu, which is impossible without a solid foundation in learning. Zhang Xiaoshi's beasts are vividly depicted. Li Zhongjie's landscapes are rigid and vigorous, and Lou Yuqing's flowers and birds are elegant and interesting. Huang Zongxiang's landscapes are victorious in ink rhyme. Sang Boyin's figures capture the true essence of Xiaomei. His younger brother Zhongming's landscapes follow Shigu. Xue Shifang's flowers resemble his teacher Jia'an very much. Tang Yifang imitates Gu Ximei's ladies, and his brushwork is quiet and solemn. Yu Yinzhan is the only female painter in this society. Her landscapes are colored and free from smoke and fire. Her calligraphy has the styles of Yu Yiweng, Song Jin, Yang Shen, Si Qi, Chen Taoyi, and Yu Luxue, all of which are like dragons and snakes flying, with strength penetrating the paper. These are all orchids in art, moved to the seaside, and emitting a unique fragrance. Moreover, there are many ancient paintings and calligraphy collected by a certain member of the Yong Society. Wandering among them is like looking at each other and smiling with artists from ancient and modern times. We urban people are immersed in red lights and green wine every day. In this sultry weather, do we want to wipe away ten buckets of vulgar dust and wash away the mounds in our hearts? Why not go there? This is a cooling and calming agent.

Little Western Paradise 179

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Fifteen: Earnest Words of Advice Without Slapping the Table in Vain; The Sound of Money and Shadows Pitifully Selling People

Jia Duocai folded his arms in front of his chest, sneered, and snorted from his nose. Yang Wanhua also put on a stern face and said, "Sister-in-law Hu, you are too ungrateful. Master Jia is spending money to marry a concubine, how can he give you a paper receipt? In front of Master Jia, I want to reveal the truth, as long as the girl passes the door and gets Master Jia's favor, then there is nothing that cannot be done." To Zhuhushi, "You should sign the paper, it's getting late, you should go back early to pack up for the girl." A full set of pens and ink were placed next to the paper. Yang Wanhua helped her up, dipped the pen in ink, and handed it to Zhu Hushi. She took the pen and kept trembling. Yang Wanhua said! "Just draw a cross, why are you trembling?" Zhu Hushi said: "Hey! Yang, once I sign, my child..." She suddenly stopped here. Cheng Zhiqian, who was outside the window, felt that these words were extremely pitiful, and could not bear to listen or watch, so he returned to his room to sit and watch. After about ten minutes, footsteps passed by on the corridor, it was Sister-in-law Hu and Zhu Hushi talking. Zhu Hushi said: "His aunt, do you think Master Jia will let us come and go in the future? Otherwise, today is killing my child. Although she is a girl, I will keep my widowhood for a lifetime, and there is no second one in front of me." He mumbled and bit, and walked over. Zhiqian couldn't bear to hear the words of this pitiful woman. Then, with a giggling sound, Zhang Jia Yang, a man and a woman, also passed by. (257)

Fragrant Shadows Record 180

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

As soon as the prescription was delivered to her hand, she hurriedly flipped through it one by one; but she saw her frowning, shaking her head, smiling, and groaning, as if she was extremely suspicious of the four prescriptions.

"This is what we dislike the most, why is it written down?" The Empress Dowager pointed to each medicine name with her finger and criticized it very casually: "This is not worth anything; this is very common, everyone knows it is used to refresh the mind, we don't want to use it either! Look at this, I don't know what it's for?"

The old eunuch, who had a thorough knowledge of various Chinese medicines, leaned over and looked at the Empress Dowager's finger. Fortunately, his eyesight was not bad. He immediately opened a medicine book and replied:

"This is for cooling the blood, back to the Old Buddha!"

"Good!" The Empress Dowager nodded and replied: "This one can be used, write it down! What does this one mean?"

She pointed out another medicine name, and the old eunuch leaned over again, looked clearly, and turned out a medicine book as evidence.

"This can clear people's heads and eyes, Empress Dowager."

When the Empress Dowager heard him say this, and looked at the medicine book, it was written in the same way, so she nodded again and waved to the eunuch in charge of writing, telling him to write down this medicine as well. (357)

New Miscellany

The Viewpoint of "Suzhou" and "Wuxi" 181

— Transferred from Tao

Along the Beijing-Shanghai railway line, there are indeed many scenic spots, and the scenery of Jiangnan can be said to be occupied by the Beijing-Shanghai railway line; in addition, in recent years, the local authorities have spared no effort in sorting out the landscape; for example, Qingyang Port and Kunshan, although they are very small areas, have become places for Chinese and Western people to visit on holidays because of the good scenery. However, strictly speaking, among the many scenic spots on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, Suzhou and Wuxi are naturally the most appreciated and praised by the general public.

The land of Qingjia in Sanwu has already told us in history. There are many ancient relics of famous people in Suzhou; the mountains and rivers and scenery are all worth praising. Looking at the poems and articles of the predecessors, I don't know how many praised Suzhou. Suzhou can be called a state of cultural relics, which is beyond doubt. Moreover, the beauty of Suzhou, good scenery is still the second, the first is quiet, that is, the residents of Suzhou also seem to be indifferent to the world; if a person can live in Suzhou for a long time, Qingfu is the most enviable. No wonder in recent years, many retired officials have to buy houses in Wuxia, which shows that Suzhou is suitable for living, and has been generally recognized. Therefore, it is more accurate to call Suzhou a residential area.

Suzhou is indeed a good place, but in my opinion: Suzhou is only suitable for living, when it comes to scenery, it should be left to Wuxi, everyone may also believe this sentence; anyone who has been to Suzhou can always know, where is the good scenery? Even the locals who grew up in Suzhou may not be able to answer; Tiger Hill can only be regarded as a mound, Tianping Mountain is just a false name, and what other mountains are worth lingering on! As for the ancient relics like Hanshan Temple, they are even more desolate and pitiful, only suitable for poets and scholars to mourn, and not to mention the scenery! The scenery of Wuxi can be called unique on the Beijing-Shanghai line. Along the Taihu Lake, Yuantouzhu, Xiaoji Mountain, Meiyuan, and Zhongyuan, which one is not as lovely as a fairyland; as for the spirit of the people of Wuxi in organizing the scenic area, it is also really admirable, and Suzhou is only one in ten thousand!

Therefore, I think: Although "Suzhou" and "Wuxi" are often referred to together, the local situation is really different. To travel and enjoy the mountains and rivers, it is better to go to Wuxi; to live, of course, Suzhou is the only one; and the "living" scope of Suzhou is also very narrow, its benefits, in addition to quietness and comfort, you can't get anything else. Someone said: "The food in Suzhou is famous far and wide, and living in Suzhou, you will always enjoy the taste of food." Oh my! I object to this sentence. Where can the food in Suzhou be compared to Wuxi? Not to mention Wuxi, even other places can't be compared, because no matter how small a place is, there will always be one or two specialties in "eating" that other places can't match. May I ask: What is Suzhou's famous specialty? Everything, although it can't be said to be bad, you can't say it's good, it's just ordinary! If you say that the dishes in Suzhou are fresh, they are still not as good as Wuxi, because the restaurants in Wuxi raise fish and shrimp in the river, how can Suzhou do that? Many Shanghai friends go to Suzhou to play, and come back dissatisfied after eating, this is an ironclad fact.

I am not despising Suzhou and praising Wuxi, but just speaking my observations.

Education News

Ministry of Education Organizes Various Universities in Sichuan Province and Decides on Six Measures to Be Followed by Telegram 182

(Nanjing, 4th) According to the results of the Ministry of Education sending personnel to inspect education in Sichuan Province, it has decided on six organizational measures for various universities and colleges in the province, and ordered Sichuan University and Sichuan Education Department to comply. (1) The Departments of Science and Education and Politics and Economics of National Sichuan University shall be merged into the various departments of the Faculty of Arts, and the Faculty of Agriculture shall be added; (2) Chongqing University shall be established as a provincial university, with the Faculties of Science and Engineering first. The original Departments of Mathematics and Physics shall be merged into the Faculty of Engineering to establish the Departments of Civil Engineering, Mining and Metallurgy, and Electrical Engineering. When funds are sufficient, the Faculty of Medicine shall be added. The students of the original Faculties of Arts and Agriculture shall be incorporated into Sichuan University; (3) The Provincial Faculty of Agriculture shall be merged into Sichuan University, and the Provincial Education Department shall take over first; (4) The Provincial Faculty of Engineering shall be merged into a major institution, and the original site and equipment shall be used by the Department to reorganize vocational schools; (5) The original students of Major University who have not been filed shall be subject to screening by the Department and submitted to the Ministry for approval; (6) The original funds of the Provincial Faculties of Agriculture and Engineering shall be allocated to Sichuan University and Major University for distribution. The affiliated middle and primary schools of Sichuan University and various universities and colleges shall be uniformly managed by the Sichuan Education Department, and the funds shall be raised separately by the Department.

Ministry of Education Instruction on Private Railway College for Strict Rectification 189

On the 4th, the Ministry of Education issued an instruction to the private Railway College, the original order roughly stating: "The college was previously prompted by the Ministry to improve according to key points. Now, according to the inspector's report, the college buildings are extremely unsuitable, there are still many teachers, the part-time salaries are meager, the students' level is low, the enrollment is excessive, the usual training is not serious, important personnel fail to take practical responsibility, various forms and statistics are mostly missing, the economic and educational situation cannot be investigated, equipment additions are extremely economical, books are still lacking, and the equipment of the attached secondary vocational classes is particularly simple. Recently, internal disputes have arisen in the college. Upon inspection of the submitted information, the college has not made any improvements regarding the Ministry's orders and prompts for the past year, and other handling situations are mostly unsuitable. It should have its establishment revoked, but it is given a final opportunity for improvement. It is temporarily ordered to suspend enrollment this year. All the following points must be strictly rectified within one year to observe the subsequent effect. The rectification situation should still be reported to the Ministry for review at any time. 1. School buildings and school equipment are not applicable and should be repaired, built, and purchased separately. 2. The accounting department of the college was approved by the Ministry to set up secondary vocational equipment. The equipment is simple and should be discontinued to concentrate efforts and enrich the content. 3. Students' coursework should be seriously assessed and training equipment must be added according to the designated funds for teaching and reference needs. 4. Teachers should still focus on full-time teachers and improve their salaries. Those who teach up to thirty hours per week should be restricted. Office staff must be vigorously rectified to improve administrative efficiency, management and hygiene, and should be improved. This order," and so on.

Teng Baiye's Opinions on Municipal Museum, Collections Should Focus on National Cultural Heritage and Efforts Should Be Made to Transplant the Tang Dynasty Murals of Dunhuang 194

The construction of the municipal museum in the city center is nearing completion. Its scale will be unique in the country. Mr. Teng Baiye, director of the Department of Fine Arts at Shanghai Hujiang University, is very familiar with the museum's situation. He has interned at the Chicago Field Museum, the New York Museum of Natural History, and the Harvard University Fogg Museum for many years. He has also visited and inspected major museums in various countries around the world and has a wealth of knowledge. He has contributed many opinions on the municipal museum. Mr. Cai Yuanpei, a director of the museum, is very satisfied and will submit them to the board of directors for adoption. The main points are recorded as follows: (1) The collection of the municipal museum should focus on the national cultural heritage. To revive the nation, it is necessary to promote the crystallization of the nation and create a kind of combined psychological symbol among the people. Moreover, the national cultural heritage will become less and less in the future. If it is not preserved, it will be exported abroad as much as possible and will not return. (2) The collection must have some items that can occupy a superior position in museums around the world, so that scholars from all over the world can come to the country to study. (3) The museum should petition the National Government to send people to Dunhuang, Gansu, to completely transplant the Tang Dynasty murals to preserve the antiquities. These murals have long been coveted by foreigners and half of them have been lost. Moreover, the local residents have limited knowledge and cause much damage. During the Russian Revolution, soldiers who fled and stayed in this area suffered looting. If there is another Russo-Japanese or world war, China will no longer have ancient murals. (The transplant method can be provided when necessary.) (4) The municipal museum should reserve the absolute sacred right of selection for the collection. The donation of individual works of art by artists or the personal collections of collectors should be considered or refused. (5) When the municipal museum has the resources to collect Western art for the purpose of providing the people with a noble and correct education in Western art, it is essential to not buy original works. Because the value of original works is very expensive, it is not within the capacity of the current national economic strength. Baiye believes that a full set of colored Western prints and plaster models of most Greek sculptures can be purchased as much as possible. (1) The value is cheap, (2) they can be freely selected, (3) they can provide the people with concrete and systematic opportunities to appreciate and educate Western art, and (4) artists who study Western painting can also learn from them. (The success of this kind of plan also requires about 100,000 yuan.) (6) Within three years of its establishment, the municipal museum should focus on mobile loan exhibitions and borrow items from domestic collectors and shops for public exhibition to prepare for purchases. (7) When the municipal museum holds exhibitions, it should display the exhibits separately according to the topic, such as ancient and modern fish painting exhibitions, Southern Song ink painting exhibitions, blue and green landscape painting exhibitions, orchid and bamboo painting exhibitions, etc., so that the public can have the opportunity to conduct systematic research and appreciation, in order to increase general knowledge and concrete appreciation. (8) The municipal museum should hold regular lectures and screenings of art films under the guidance of the Municipal Education Bureau. (9) The municipal museum should cooperate with the Antiquities Preservation Association to investigate and register the Chinese cultural relics scattered abroad. (Baiye can provide 50% of the materials, as he has taken this as his responsibility when he was abroad.) (10) The municipal museum should cooperate with the provincial governments to excavate antiquities for preservation. (11) The municipal museum should ask the Academia Sinica for donations of some of the antiquities they excavated from the ruins. (12) The municipal museum can borrow some cultural relics from the Palace Museum, either for three years or one year, rotating borrowing and returning them for the research of the people of Shanghai. (13) The municipal museum should contact collectors abroad, borrow and exhibit each other, or exchange collections, or purchase or exchange important representative treasures of our country scattered abroad. (14) The municipal museum should cooperate with art schools to restore various kinds of old Chinese arts that have been lost or are about to be lost, such as printing, lacquer painting, bamboo carving, jade carving, etc. (15) The municipal museum should have air humidity and temperature control. (16) The municipal museum should hire specialized personnel to be in charge of exhibition matters. This work seems easy, but it is very difficult to do well. Hanging pictures all over the wall cannot be called a good exhibition. The hanging of a painting, high or low, near or far, is closely related to the ink color, newness, size, mounting, and light, as well as the walls and colors of the neighboring paintings. (The cluttered hanging of the London pre-exhibition is ridiculed by professionals.) (17) The walls of the municipal museum should be earth gray, and the floors and other wood materials should be light brown Phoebe nanmu. Otherwise, it will inevitably lead to a counterproductive result. The word "simple" is the highest theory in art.

Sports Expert Zhang Jiwu Talks About His Impressions of Overseas Inspection, Germany Uses Sports Training Instead of Military Training, Sports are Very Popular in Various Countries as Part of Daily Life, China's Sports are Still in a Distorted State of Development 201

Zhang Jiwu, the director of physical education at Nankai University in Tianjin, went abroad during the summer of 1933 to specialize in physical education and examine the status of sports facilities in various European and American countries. He obtained a master's degree in physical education from the German National Institute and was also very concerned about the social, economic, political, and educational aspects of various countries. He originally intended to conduct further research and inspection, but due to his wife's serious illness, he returned to the country on the Japanese Empress wheel on the evening of the 2nd and stayed at the New Asia Hotel. He socialized with colleagues in the sports world in Shanghai and visited the newly built municipal stadium. He then took a train north on the night of the 3rd. When asked about his impressions of this trip, Mr. Zhang briefly described the general situation due to the suddenness of the time. The narration is as follows:

Overseas Experience

After going abroad, Mr. Zhang first went to Germany and entered the German National Academy of Physical Education, specializing in the study of physical education administration and social sports. Then he went to various European countries for inspection. After a year, he went to the United States for inspection. He spent a total of one year in Europe and one year in the United States. On the way back to the country, he stayed in Japan for a short time. Due to time constraints, he was unable to conduct a thorough inspection. He obtained a master's degree in physical education from the German Sports Academy. He participated in the doctoral degree examination in the United States, but he did not submit the thesis in time because of the news of his wife's illness, so he waited to return to the country. He continued to write after returning to the country, and then he would send the manuscript to the United States.

German Sports

German sports emphasizes society first, followed by schools. Under the jurisdiction of Fathesti, the organization is very thorough. Regardless of men, women, old or young, all must receive physical training. Especially after the European War, Germany was deeply oppressed by various countries, such as restricting armaments and not allowing military training. President Hitler, in view of this, forced the implementation of physical training. The methods of physical training include not only practicing gymnastics and various sports, but also including knowledge related to military affairs. Therefore, people from all walks of life in the country can exercise and have military knowledge. It is called physical training, but it is actually military training, and its effect is even greater than that of independent military training, and it will not be interfered with by various countries. Once the country is in trouble, the people of the whole country will be able to sacrifice themselves to defend the country.

Italy, etc.

Italy's sports are completely important in the social aspect. Mussolini attaches great importance to physical training. After work hours, people must go to the sports field. All sports administration is presided over by the government. Regarding the attendance of athletes at the 1936 World Games, Mussolini has ordered active training to win glory for the country. Finland specializes in social sports. Almost none of the athletes attending the World Games are students. Denmark, Sweden, and other countries still adhere to the old methods, focusing on soft gymnastics. The domestic people in the United States are very familiar with physical education, and social and schools are equally important. The athlete system is particularly valued. Japan is similar to the situation in the United States, but special attention is paid to elementary school physical education. Every elementary school is very perfect in terms of physical education facilities and administration. Russia specializes in social sports, which is presided over by the Communist Party. The promotion is very strong and has spread throughout the country. As soon as people have free time, they go to the sports field to participate in activities.

Thoughts and Feelings

Mr. Zhang also talked about his many thoughts on domestic education. Our country's sports emphasize schools and neglect society. People still regard sports as unimportant. If sports rely solely on schools to promote, it is the most passive method. For example, building a great stadium is only for the purpose of opening a sports meeting, and the meaning does not seem to be very profound. Sports fields are lined up everywhere abroad, but there is still a problem of overcrowding. This is because sports have been popularized, and there is a need for more sports fields to induce exercise. The idea is not undesirable, but it is ultimately a distorted phenomenon. Therefore, in the domestic situation, the first step is to start from the bottom level, and then we should try to link the upper and lower level work together. If so, the results can be faster.

News of the Tokyo Table Tennis Team's Visit to Shanghai: Our Local Table Tennis Community Prepares to Respond 205

The Tokyo Table Tennis League, recognizing the increasing development of table tennis in our country and the considerable combat power in terms of skills, invited our team to Japan in the spring of the 16th year of the Republic, due to the Shanghai Chinese team's renowned reputation. As a result, our country defeated Japan's strongest Osaka Kota Spinning Factory team with a superior score of four to one, which was widely reported in newspapers, shocking the entire country. Although our country suffered a disastrous defeat in the Far Eastern Games demonstration match later, the Japanese people's belief in and fear of our players' skills remained unchanged, regarding us as Japan's imaginary enemy, practicing diligently day and night, all with the goal of being able to defeat our country, as if there could be no greater honor. Therefore, the planning of the Japanese team's expedition to Shanghai never ceased. Due to international trends, the event was suspended. Now, they plan to take advantage of the summer vacation in August to travel across the ocean for an experimental exploration, to fulfill their ambition. Their ambition is so great that it is no different from annexing mountains and rivers. The greatness of their spiritual and financial sacrifice can be seen here. Therefore, our country's table tennis authorities should plan ahead, prepare their troops, and have proper plans to counter strong enemies in order to protect international glory. Because this matter is of great importance, a meeting must be convened to discuss the organization, selection, training, and combat arrangement of Shanghai's elite players with a spirit of collective wisdom and effort, so that there may be hope of victory against the formidable enemy.

The July contract had already broken through the 2-yuan barrier. At a time when spot cotton inventories were abundant, this squeeze was actually occurring. In fact, after a long period of decline, once a rebound occurs, it is temporarily difficult to relax.

Grains: Spot Foreign Wheat Dumped at Low Prices, Futures Flour Wheat Rises and Falls Back, Bran Stockpiles Thicken Daily at Mills 215

The flour market rose and then fell, and the market sentiment was mixed. Although foreign wheat was quoted at small prices from 48 cents to 1.20 yuan, and the weather had cleared up, the floodwaters in the Yangtze River area had not receded. Although the mills had seen smooth sales the previous day, they stopped afterwards. Therefore, the opening prices for all months rose by about one cent. By the afternoon opening, all months turned down again, especially the distant months. Furthermore, the dumping of spot foreign wheat became increasingly rampant. Fu'ao wheat was quoted at only 4.52 yuan, resulting in a large volume of selling. Many bulls also unloaded their positions, falling by nearly 1-2 cents compared to the morning closing price, and distant months falling by 3-4 cents. Observing the subsequent movements, there is a fear that changes may still occur due to foreign wheat. As a result, the current month was unchanged, August fell by 1 cent, September fell by 1.5 cents, October fell by 0.5 cents, November fell by 2 cents, and December fell by 2.25 cents.

The wheat market opened in the morning with a rather positive sentiment. Because foreign wheat fluctuated very slightly and gold prices also had little change, brokers, considering that floodwaters had not receded in various places and fearing that deliveries would be obstructed, saw active standard buying. The current month was up 5-6 cents from the previous day. Distant months, however, were affected by the dumping of spot foreign wheat, and sentiment was also weak. Observing the dull situation in subsequent trading, there is a fear that it will be broken again by foreign wheat. As a result, the current month rose by 3 cents, August was unchanged, September fell by 1 cent, and October fell by 2 cents. Spot wheat was raised by 3-4 cents due to mills releasing shipments of ship wheat. Train wheat was not taken up for other reasons. It was heard that Zhenjiang wheat from Wai Tu was 3.41 yuan, Danyang wheat was 3.41 yuan, second-grade wheat was 3.06 yuan, Yangzhou wheat was 3.42 yuan, second-grade wheat was 3.40 yuan, Daqiao wheat was 3.45 yuan, Zhitang wheat was 3.46 yuan, Benniu wheat was 3.44 yuan, Guandian Mingguang wheat was 3.49 yuan, Yanghe Chuzhou wheat was 3.47 yuan, Kunshan wheat was 3.45-3.46 yuan, and Penglai wheat was 3.42-3.44 yuan. The bran market has been in a state of sluggishness for a long time. The purchasing power in the inland is really thin, and the prices of various commodities have been falling continuously. As a result, most farmers who use it as feed have stopped buying, and the mills' stockpiles have been thickening step by step. Therefore, the current asking price has fallen to as low as 1.93-1.94 yuan.
